  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=8.9)
    The forgotten library inside a pyramid creates an immersive, atmospheric setting perfectly suited to the story's tone and concept. The sensory details are exceptional—dust sighing, echoes fluttering between scrolls, moonlight piercing a collapsed skylight. The pyramid's acoustics shifting "like turning tides" brilliantly connects setting to action. The atmosphere masterfully supports both the character's phobias and the "mundanely spiritual" quality, creating a haunting yet grounded ambiance that feels vital to the narrative.
